This file is a text copy of the css created and cached. It is presented for reference for any user wishing to
disable LESS on the fly during development.
There is no purpose to editing this file as it is a text readme file and not an active part of the theme.
Copy the css below and save as base.css, then add that to the theme config.php and remove the LESS lines.
/****************************************************************************************************************/

/* Copy of entire css used when turning LESS compiling off during development
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */

}

    display: none;
    height: 0;

    display: none;
